With Rich Peach Blossom Flavor, Xu Qizhong's Bankruptcy Meeting 124

Creditors Include Dance Hall Owners with Special Connections, Assets Include Clothing Valued at Over Four Thousand Yuan

Xu Qizhong, the 22-year-old son of Wu Xing's wealthy merchant Xu Guannan, who resides at No. 61 North Zhejiang Road in Shanghai, recently declared bankruptcy to the First Special District Court, claiming that he was unable to repay the huge debt of over 31,000 yuan for dance expenses, high-end restaurant bills, travel expenses, fashion, cosmetics, and other expenses owed to Saint Anna, Paramount, Atlantic, Jinlong, Daxia, He Han, Hongxiang, Sincere, and other businesses. The court accepted the case, and a creditors' meeting was convened yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. The Datong News Agency reporter has recorded the details of the situation as follows:

Creditors Present

The creditors' meeting yesterday was held at the original location of the China Industrial Bank on the third floor of Nanjing Road. More than 20 people attended, including representatives from Li Han Car Rental, Sincere Department Store, Jinlong Western Restaurant, Paramount Hotel, Atlantic Hotel, Gaohe Women's Shoe Store, as well as Shen Liang (i.e., Mr. Hu), Ying Huizhen (brothel owner), and others. The debtor, Xu Qizhong, also attended the meeting.

Chairman's Report

The meeting was chaired by the prosecutor Yu Lude and supervisor Wang Sifang, both accountants, appointed by the First Special District Court. The clerk of the First Special District Court, Ying Yeping, served as the recorder. First, prosecutor Yu announced the purpose of the meeting and inquired about the debtor Xu Qizhong's age and occupation. The response was that he was 22 years old, unemployed, and had previously studied at school. Then, accountant Shan Wang reported that the total amount of declared claims was 31,866 yuan, while the amount of claims present at the meeting today was only 3,416 yuan and 19 cents.

Meeting Proceedings

After the reporting matters were completed, the discussion began. The creditor Ying Huizhen spoke first, stating that she had lent the debtor a total of 10,000 yuan in installments, all with promissory notes issued by the debtor. However, when questioning the debtor, he admitted to only borrowing 1,000 yuan, claiming that the promissory notes issued were for a special circumstance and were fictitious, which led to considerable dispute between the two parties. Then, the creditor Zhao Congyan from Li Han Car Rental spoke, citing Article 156 of the Bankruptcy Law, stating that the debtor owed the Atlantic Restaurant 1,000 yuan in dining expenses, the Daxia Car Rental Company 1,500 yuan in transportation expenses, and the Paramount and Saint Anna dance halls hundreds of yuan each, which clearly met the conditions of Article 1, which states, "Wasteful gambling or other speculative behavior that obviously reduces property," and has actually violated the criminal law.

Overview of Liabilities

Finally, prosecutor Yu persuaded both parties to make concessions and negotiated a compromise plan based on the reconciliation plan proposed by the debtor on the spot, pending a decision at the second creditors' meeting. Then, Zhao Congyan, Le Junze, and Ying Huizhen were elected as auditors, and the meeting was adjourned. The following is an excerpt from the liabilities and assets that have been declared, as recorded by accountant Wang Sifang: 1. (Liabilities) Atlantic Restaurant 1,000 yuan, Daxia Car Rental Company 1,500 yuan, Mingxiang Fashion Company 500 yuan, Paramount Hotel 100 yuan, Jinlong Restaurant 150 yuan, as well as Saint Anna Dance Hall, Ying Huizhen, etc., totaling 31,866 yuan. 2. (Assets) Chinese and Western clothing valued at 1,800 yuan (original price 4,320 yuan), a Studebaker car valued at 800 yuan (original price 8,599 yuan), a Capehart long and short wave radio-phonograph, complete with automatic record changer, record player, and film projector, valued at 250 yuan (original price 5,500 yuan), a Northern Electric refrigerator valued at 100 yuan (original price 850 yuan), totaling an estimated value of 3,033 yuan (original price 26,399 yuan, 14 cents).

Education News

National Scout Grand Review Provincial and Municipal Participation Methods 135

The Basic Unit is the Regiment as the Smallest Unit

——Exceptions for Remote Provinces and Cities——

The second National Scout Grand Review and Jamboree of the China Scout General Association was originally scheduled to be held in the capital last October. However, due to the Ministry of Finance's funds not being allocated, it was indefinitely postponed. The association has now received all the funds approved by the central government and has also received them from the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, it has begun to prepare according to the original plan and is scheduled to be officially held in the capital on October 10th of this year. The methods for participation by provinces and cities have also been formulated, and the local councils were instructed yesterday to prepare as soon as possible and to fill in the exact number of participating scouts from the date of receipt of the order to the end of May, and report them, etc. It has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. The participation methods are recorded below:

Notice of Participation: The General Association yesterday issued a notice to all councils stating, "In order to comply with orders, after reviewing the Association's decision to hold the second National Scout Grand Review and Jamboree in the capital on the Double Tenth Festival this year, it has been submitted to the central government for approval. A special order is issued with participation methods and registration forms, which should be jointly forwarded by the association, the party headquarters, and the education authorities to their subordinates to prepare as soon as possible, and from the date of receipt of the order to the end of May, fill in the exact number of participating scouts and report them for verification. Please comply with this order."

Participation Methods: Participation methods for the second National Scout Grand Review and Jamboree of the China Scout General Association: Participating units: The Association calculates participating units by province and city. Each province and city must recommend one general leader to be solely responsible. As for the basic unit, it is stipulated that the regiment formed in accordance with item 4 shall be the standard. Those with less than one regiment shall not attend. For example, if Province A has twenty regiments and one company, only twenty regiments can attend, and this one company, which is less than one regiment, cannot send anyone to attend. Also, if Province B is one company and Province C is one squad, then this one company and squad cannot attend, because the basic unit of attendance is the regiment as the smallest unit (but border provinces can be accommodated). Each province and city must first allocate and arrange according to the organization in item 4 after the Association has verified the number of people, so as to avoid temporary confusion. However, the original regimental flags of each regiment, even after the various regiments have been mixed to form a new organization, must still be brought for review. People selection: Those who have obtained badges above the elementary level (border provinces can be accommodated). Number of people: Each province and city shall stipulate its own selection methods and shall submit the exact number of participants to the Association for verification from the date of receipt of the order to the end of May (if a scout leaves the regiment before the review and cannot attend, they shall not be included). Temporary organization for the review and jamboree: Seven to nine people are a squad, including the squad leader and deputy squad leader. Six squads are a company. Three companies are a regiment. Those with less than one regiment may form a regiment by mixing various units before they can participate.

Review Location: The registration form stipulates the following: General Leader, Deputy Leader (indicate Boy Scout or Girl Scout), Coach (indicate Boy Scout or Girl Scout), Service Personnel and Coaches, Boy Scouts (organized as follows: Regiment, Company, Squad, Number of people with elementary badges), Campsite (bell-shaped or house-shaped). As for the review location, according to news from the General Association, it has been generally decided to be in the area of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum and the Central Stadium, etc. A careful survey will still need to be conducted recently to make the final decision.

National Children's Year Implementation Association Hosts National Children's Teaching Aids and Toys Exhibition 142

The Municipal Education Bureau Collects Products from the City on Behalf of the Association. Deadline: March 5th to the Bureau for Transfer.

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued instructions to municipal and private registered primary schools and social education organizations and cultural groups in this city, stating, "With reference to the official letter Er Zi No. 431 of February 5, 25, from the National Children's Year Implementation Association, the Association, in accordance with the provisions of the Outline of Implementation Methods for Children's Year, will hold a National Children's Teaching Aids and Toys Exhibition in April of this year. Enclosed is a copy of the Association's methods, which you are requested to follow the third item of the methods and send to the Association before March 15th for display and exhibition. Accordingly, it is hereby notified for your information and action, etc., and a copy of the original methods of the National Children's Teaching Aids and Toys Exhibition is enclosed. You are hereby ordered to select and send products to the Bureau before March 5th for transfer without delay. Be sure to follow this order." The methods of the National Children's Teaching Aids and Toys Exhibition are as follows: The purpose of this Association: (1) To arouse the attention of people in society to teaching aids and toys. (2) To encourage the imitation and creation of teaching aids and toys. (3) To seek the improvement of teaching aids and toys. (4) The exhibits shall be mainly domestic products and may also selectively display foreign products at the same time for reference. (5) The domestic exhibits will be collected by the National Children's Year Implementation Association from schools, stores, and factories across the country. The reference products will be requested by the Association from the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order embassies and consulates abroad to solicit them from the governments of the United States, Germany, Britain, Russia, France, Italy, and Japan. (6) The National Children's Year Implementation Association will hire personnel who have researched primary school teaching aids and children's toys to be judges and evaluate the quality of the products. The standards for judging teaching aids and toys are as follows: (1) Educational value. (2) Creative nature. (3) In line with science or containing scientific meaning. (4) Sufficient to arouse children's martial spirit (specifically for toys). (5) Sanitary. (6) Strong and durable. (7) The National Children's Year Implementation Association will publish the results of the evaluation in the newspaper one month after the closing of the exhibition and publish a booklet for reference. (8) The National Children's Year Implementation Association will request the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry to commend particularly excellent products. (9) All proceedings of this Association shall be jointly handled by the National Children's Year Implementation Association and the Ministry of Education. (10) The expenses of this Association shall be provided by the National Children's Year Implementation Association and the Ministry of Education. (11) The exhibition period of this Association is ten days, from April of the 25th to the 14th. (11) After the exhibition has been held, the exhibits of this Association may be transported to the requested locations for touring display upon request from provinces and cities, but all expenses shall be borne by the requester. (12) At the end of the National Children's Year Implementation Association, the exhibits shall be disposed of separately. Those who request the return of the exhibits beforehand shall be returned immediately. Those who do not want to be returned shall be established as a permanent museum for preservation. (13) The local Children's Year Implementation Committees may refer to these methods and formulate other methods for holding teaching aids and toy exhibitions. The local exhibitions may select one of the two types of teaching aids and toys to hold the exhibition. (14) These methods shall be reviewed and implemented by the Standing Committee of the National Children's Year Implementation Association.

Children's Education Novel

Little Men (1) (7) (8) 146

—Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Mr. Bhaer was deeply moved by Mrs. Bergmann's kindness and warm words, so he asked the children: "Are you willing to go?" "We are," they replied in unison. An hour later, led by Franz, they went to participate in John Brooke's simple funeral, performing their duties as part of the group.

The small house looked quiet, comfortable, and full of sunlight, just like when Meg entered as a bride ten years ago. However, at that time, it was early summer, and roses were in full bloom everywhere. Now it is autumn, and the withered yellow leaves fell rustling in the wind, making the branches on the trees even more bleak. The bride is now a widow, but that same quiet beauty still shone on her face. The solemn beauty of a devout person who has suddenly encountered a great disaster, knows that it cannot be saved, and can console themselves, directly comforted those who came to mourn.

"Ah, Meg! What kind of cultivation do you have that enables you to endure this so much?" Shu said to her softly, because she came to the door to greet them, revealing some well-intentioned smiles of invitation, and did not change her usual gentle demeanor, but was even more gentle.

"Dear Shu, the love that has made me happy for the past ten years is still my support. It will not die out. I now feel that John is even more mine," Meg said softly. In her eyes, a kind of gentle confidence was so clear and beautiful that Shu could not help but believe her and feel that the immortality of love was like what she possessed, and truly thank God for the gift.

Page 16

Economic Supplement

The Success of Bond Consolidation 147

— Tan Bingwen

Our national finances have generally suffered from annual deficits of approximately 140 to 150 million yuan over the past five to six years (with the deficit reaching a staggering 217 million yuan in the 19th year of the Republic). In addition to increasing new taxes, the government has resorted to raising debt to fill the gap. Before the 16th year of the Republic, foreign debt exceeded domestic debt. Thereafter, domestic debt increased while foreign borrowing ceased, which is a symbolic indication of progress in our nation's debt policy. According to the "Financial Yearbook of the Ministry of Finance" (published in September of the 24th year of the Republic), as of the 15th year of the Republic, domestic debt totaled 381,166,243 yuan, and foreign debt totaled 3,034,961,374 yuan. Compared to the total amount of public debt, the former accounted for 11.15%, and the latter for 88.85%. From the 16th year to the 21st year of the Republic, the amount of debt raised totaled 1,256,915,864 yuan for domestic debt, accounting for 90.77%, and only 30,729,045 yuan for foreign debt, accounting for 9.23%. From the 22nd year of the Republic, the amount of debt raised totaled 549,591,413 yuan for domestic debt, accounting for 89.55%; and 64,000,000 yuan for foreign debt, accounting for 10.45%. Raising our debt, whether domestic or foreign, is not without its drawbacks from both an economic and political perspective. Therefore, it should not be attempted unless there is no other way to increase internal and external debt. Now that the amount of foreign debt being raised is gradually decreasing, the "dependency" of our nation's economy and politics is also gradually disappearing. Therefore, I believe this is a positive phenomenon.

However, borrowing is truly just a short-term fix, like "eating this year's harvest to cover next year's needs." To balance the national economy, expenditures must equal revenues, and issuing public debt is often unavoidable. Even when issuing domestic debt, the people's ability to bear the burden and the impact on the entire national economy must be considered. Otherwise, it could lead to a situation that harms the people and wastes resources. What is the reality in our country? Please see the table on the left: (Based on Wang Zongpei's "Inland Public Debt in the Past Month," Bank Weekly, Volume 20, Issue 3.) The unit for the issued amount is in millions of yuan, except where indicated as yuan.

What is noteworthy in the table is that no public debt was issued in the 21st year of the Republic. This was likely not due to a balanced budget, but rather because the public debt market had reached a point of saturation. Furthermore, looking at the accumulated balance at the end of each year, it increases rapidly every year except for the 6 million yuan decrease in the 21st year. In the 24th year, it increased by nearly 300 million yuan compared to the 23rd year. In today's era where everything needs to be rebuilt, we are not surprised by the expansion of public debt. However, debt must be repaid. According to the declaration issued by the bondholder association on February 1st, as of the end of January of this year, the government still owed a total of over 1.46 billion yuan in various domestic public bonds, treasury bills, certificates, etc., with a massive monthly payment of over 15 million yuan for principal and interest. Consequently, the proportion of debt service in national fiscal expenditure is increasing day by day. If the finances are tight, more public debt will be issued; if more public debt is issued, the financial difficulties will worsen. Isn't this a difficult situation for financial management?

(Note) The unit is in thousands of yuan. For years before the 22nd year of the Republic, the figures are based on the final accounts of the Ministry of Finance. For the 23rd and 24th years, they are based on the budgeted amounts.

With the increase in debt service on the expenditure side, it is inevitable that more new debt must be borrowed to facilitate turnover. According to the financial yearbook and the statistical materials released by the Ministry of Finance, the income from borrowing funds and the percentage of the total annual income are as shown in the table on the left.

(Note) The unit is in thousands of yuan. For years before the 22nd year of the Republic, the figures are based on the final accounts of the Ministry of Finance. For the 23rd and 24th years, they are based on the budgeted amounts.

By comparing the second and third tables, we can see that borrowing only increases financial difficulties. Debt accounts for more than 30% of expenditures, while income from borrowing only accounts for 20%. It is truly a case of not being worth the cost.

The expansion of public debt not only offers no benefits to finances, but its detrimental impact on industry and commerce is also very obvious. Although the face value interest rates on previously issued public debt were not high, they were often sold at a discount, resulting in actual interest rates as high as 1.2% or even higher. Speculators, attracted by the high interest rates, were actively involved in the securities market. Investors, also enticed by the doubled interest rates, disregarded other types of investments. Under these circumstances, a large amount of social capital flowed into the securities market, and industry and commerce felt a severe shortage of funds, leaving them unable to inject capital and leading to today's depressed state. Therefore, for the sake of consolidating finances and rescuing industry and commerce, it is necessary to reorganize the existing public debt system.

There are only two ways to reorganize: one is to contract public debt, and the other is to extend the repayment period and reduce interest rates. At a time when construction has just begun and foreign troubles are pressing, contracting public debt is difficult to achieve. Extending the repayment period and reducing interest rates was implemented once in the 21st year of the Republic, and it did not have a detrimental impact on securities credit. Implementing it again this time should not cause any major problems. Extending the repayment period will relatively reduce the government's debt service. However, from another perspective, it will affect the ability to issue debt in the future. Extending the repayment period is nothing more than shifting today's burden to tomorrow. Therefore, for the sake of planning ahead, we should strive to economize in the future as a basis for contracting public debt. If public debt is issued in the future, and is used for construction projects, then because the projects themselves can generate profits, there is no need to worry about repaying the principal and interest. If public debt is issued merely to make up for financial shortfalls, then repaying the principal and interest in the future may be more difficult. As for the issue of interest rate reduction, there is much debate. I believe that although reducing interest rates may temporarily cause some losses for bondholders, it is not only harmless but also beneficial to the entire national economy. Why is that? Lower interest rates lighten the government's debt burden, eliminating the need to increase taxes or issue more public debt to increase revenue. This is one aspect. Also, those who used to invest in securities because of the high interest rates will not be willing to do so in the future, so that capital can flow to the industrial sector. This is the second aspect. "A small lack of patience can ruin a great plan." Wise people will naturally know what to choose and what to discard, without the need for us to elaborate.

Regarding the issue of guarantees for the repayment of principal and interest on public debt, the unified public debt issued this time still follows the original provisions of the existing bonds, allocating the remaining tax revenue from customs duties after deducting indemnity payments to foreign debt for payment. However, the principal and interest of the 340 million yuan of the Reconstruction Public Debt will have to wait until after the tax revenue from customs duties has been allocated to indemnity payments to foreign debt, the long-term financial public debt of the 17th year, and the unified public debt of the 25th year, with the remaining tax revenue as the fund. As for the annual principal and interest to be repaid, taking only the unified public debt as an example, excluding the one installment of principal and interest (July 31st) paid in the 25th year, the amount of principal and interest to be repaid every five years is listed below (in units of thousands of yuan).

(Note) The year of full repayment is the amount of a single principal and interest payment. The years with the most principal and interest repayment, when the repayment is completed in the 49th year, will reach more than 14.9 million yuan, with an average of always over 10 million yuan. The principal and interest of the Reconstruction Public Debt are not included. However, since its debt amount is comparable to the unified C debt (the unified C debt is 350 million yuan), the annual principal and interest repayment can also be compared to the figures for the unified C debt (see table 2), and the national customs duties are listed below. (Unit: yuan)

The speculative activity in our country's public debt is unmatched by other countries. Examining the reasons, it is likely due to the government's lax control. Regarding this point, refer to the U.S. Securities Act of 1933 and the Exchange Speculation Control Act of 1934, and formulate the Chinese Securities Control Regulations in light of our nation's realities. I once introduced the two U.S. bills in issues 59 and 64 of this publication, in the articles "New Changes in American Securities Investment" and "New Progress in American Securities Control." The main methods are nothing more than cracking down on futures trading, strictly regulating the qualifications and scope of activities of brokers, increasing margin requirements, and regularly inspecting the books and other records of brokers and exchanges. If the above points can be applied properly, speculative activities can naturally be stopped, and legitimate investors will not be hindered at the same time.

Is There a Turnaround for the French Franc? 148

— Jiang Yusheng

(1)

In the global currency struggle, the French franc, which has been in an absolutely passive position, has recently shown signs of gradually stabilizing. On February 6th, the discount rate of the Bank of France was reduced from 5% to 2.5%. The reasons for this are: first, the French franc's exchange rate is strong. Over the past month, it has risen considerably in terms of the US dollar, and it has been very stable in terms of the British pound. Second, the movement of US cash into France, which has reached 14 million US dollars as of February 7th. Third, a large amount of domestic private reserves of hard currency have flowed back into the market due to the threat of devaluation, all of which have given France the opportunity to lower its discount rate. Therefore, it is believed that this move by France is sufficient to increase the confidence of domestic citizens and foreign speculators in French politics, dispel rumors of British loans, and indicate a turnaround for the French franc. Examining the facts and analyzing them, we know that all of this is just a kind of reaction of social psychology, and the French franc has its fundamental crisis.

(2)

The discount rate of the Bank of France has changed as many as six times in six months. The French financial community today is like a bird startled by the twang of a bow, and is most easily disturbed. If there is no solid foundation, then the current reduction in the discount rate will also be fleeting and will not help the overall situation. Once the above three reasons for the rate reduction are investigated, they are not enough to guarantee the current situation. Because the French franc is under pressure from the pound sterling, it is about to collapse. And Britain and the United States are afraid that its collapse will affect the safety of the pound sterling. Therefore, Britain and the United States have provided assistance in the past month. Britain has purchased gold in the London market to maintain the French franc, and is eager to stabilize the exchange rate between the British and French currencies at 75.06 French francs per pound sterling. The United States is shipping out gold and lowering the US dollar in order to raise the exchange rate of the French franc. All of this means that the French franc has achieved temporary stability under the control of the pound sterling, giving the French people a kind of psychological comfort. In fact, the amount of gold shipped into France by the United States last week was not as much as the amount shipped to London by France; in addition, although the amount of domestic currency flow has increased, it has not helped the international position of the French franc. Therefore, the foundation for the stability of the French franc this time is extremely fragile, and turning to consider its crisis, it is becoming more and more profound.

(3)

The fundamental crisis of the French franc lies in the fact that the pound sterling, with its exchange rate advantage, has broken the line of the gold standard group. This has caused France's foreign trade to decline rapidly. There is no room for competition abroad, and it is subject to dumping of foreign goods at home. The sharp decline in the total amount of trade over the years and the sharp increase in excess labor have both created a one-sided trend, causing domestic prices to fall, industry and commerce to decline, and capital to flee. On January 10 of this year, the reserve amount of the Bank of France was 66,267 million French francs, a decrease of 15,748 million French francs compared with the same period last year. Although the government has implemented a strict austerity policy to tide over the many difficulties, the result has made the economic situation even more depressed and the French franc's illness has become more and more profound. Therefore, when talking about the future of the French franc today, we must start from this point. The temporary import of gold and the reduction of interest rates are all trivial issues and are not enough to talk about a turnaround. If the French franc problem still needs to seek remedial measures, France really only has two ways to follow at this time: the immediate solution is to negotiate a loan from Britain; the fundamental solution is to improve the devaluation of the French franc by half. However, the French people have learned a historical lesson. After the war, it was once devalued and suffered great damage. There is a psychological fear of currency. All previous cabinets have taken maintaining the French franc as a prerequisite, and it is difficult to change the parity. However, today, times have changed, and the general trend is that we firmly believe that the French franc will be the initiator of the world's currency reset movement, and the time will not be too far away.

Discussion on Organizing Urban and Rural Banks 149

— Yu Xun

Recently, in the improvement of financial organizations, there has been discussion about setting up urban and rural banks. Regarding this point, we believe that attention should be paid. If the methods are appropriate and the facilities are appropriate, it can help the development of the rural economy and improve agricultural production and the livelihood of farmers. If the method is not appropriate, or if there is no consistent and comprehensive policy, it may only strengthen the oppression of agricultural capital by commercial capital, and even open the door for local tyrants and wealthy people to exploit farmers. Therefore, several points are originally proposed for discussion below, to help negotiate.

1. Capital Issue

The urban and rural areas we are talking about refer to the inland areas far away from big cities. As for the areas near the big cities, banks are lined up and the financial organization is actually very complete. The organization of urban and rural banks is not important. Therefore, the urban and rural banks we are talking about have the meaning of belonging to remote inland areas. Only in these areas, where economic development is still in its infancy and the financial organization is not yet complete, does the organization of urban and rural banks make sense. In these areas, the organization of banks, the capital item, has become a special problem. As a result of the economic panic in recent years, in some inland cities, business is depressed, freight is stagnant, not only is there no accumulation of funds, but most of them are heavily in debt and unable to extricate themselves. Under this kind of environment, it is actually difficult to raise funds locally in some areas. Even if it can be barely collected, the amount is very small. It will not have any effect economically. Therefore, it is actually difficult to raise capital from local merchants and people. Secondly, it is even more difficult and dangerous for local government offices to allocate funds to open. First, the credit of local government offices is the worst in the eyes of merchants and people. Raising funds by local government offices will inevitably come from compulsory means. Second, financial institutions opened by local government offices often become a tool for raising funds in finance. In today's situation where local finances are generally insufficient, it is really dangerous. I am afraid that credit cannot be established and it will disrupt finance. As for issuing bank stocks and selling them in cities, absorbing the funds of big cities, it is even more difficult in today's underdeveloped bill market. It is even more difficult to establish it by the state. At present, the country does not have such great power and energy. So urban and rural banks. It seems simple, but in fact the capital problem. It is not easy to solve. Because it is not easy to solve, the problem of land securities has emerged recently. In fact, in addition to land, there is nothing else in rural areas. Therefore, to organize a bank in rural areas and collect capital on its own, there is no way other than to base it on land. Organizing a bank based on land has become another kind of nature, and we cannot dwell on it here. In short, the capital problem of the organization of urban and rural banks seems simple, but it is actually very difficult to solve. We cannot make any specific suggestions here, but we put forward several principles as follows:

First, the capital of urban and rural banks cannot be obtained by compulsory apportionment and borrowing by local government offices.

Second, the capital of urban and rural banks should be quite strong, and cannot be nominal.

Third, the capital of urban and rural banks cannot be monopolized by local wealthy people and become a private tool.

Fourth, the capital of urban and rural banks should be of an active nature, and cannot be used as illiquid land or real estate.

Fifth, the capital of urban and rural banks should avoid being directly supplied by local government offices as much as possible.

2. Management Issues

Who manages the urban and rural banks, and who supervises them? This is also an important issue, which is closely related to the bank's credibility among the people. In theory, it is managed by the shareholders' meeting, operated by the board of directors, and supervised by the board of supervisors. This seems to be a common practice. However, since we oppose the urban and rural banks being controlled by a few financial groups, the shareholders will inevitably be dispersed. Moreover, in various places, the people are ignorant and the power of the government offices is great. The so-called urban and rural banks are actually easily manipulated by local bureaucrats and bullies, thus causing various evil dramas of embezzlement and damaging credibility. Therefore, the management problem of urban and rural banks is particularly worthy of study. In this regard, we suggest the following principles:

First, the directors of urban and rural banks should be purely commercial talents. They are absolutely prohibited from having relationships with government factories, and they are not allowed to engage in similar businesses.

Second, the content of the operation of urban and rural banks should be public and announced monthly, absolutely avoiding confidential actions. Urban and rural banks are local public banks, and the operation policy does not need to be secret.

Third, the board of directors, shareholders' meeting or board of supervisors should absolutely avoid direct relationships with local government offices. Except for being supervised by law, there is no relationship with local government offices.

Fourth, the business policy is directly supervised by the Ministry of Finance or the National Economic Commission. The business situation should also be reported to the Ministry of Finance and the National Economic Commission monthly.

The above points are to ensure that urban and rural banks are purely economic organizations and absolutely reject the intrusion of political or financial forces. The evil consequences of the unhealthy relationship between local finance and local banks have rich experience in our country. In the future, only by adopting a decisive policy can the safety of this kind of bank be guaranteed.

3. Business Issues

What kind of business do urban and rural banks operate? This is the central topic of our discussion on the issue of urban and rural banks. If the establishment of urban and rural banks is only to sell public bonds for the central or local government, sell aviation lottery tickets, or even collect taxes and borrow money for the government, then we dare to assert that it will become a tool of exploitation, which will not only be of no benefit to rural areas, but will also accelerate its collapse. We do not hope to organize such urban and rural banks. In the past, China set up many banks for agriculture, industry, commerce, industry, and domestic goods, but the results were not true to their names, and everyone embarked on the road of public bond trading. In the end, no one cared about the industry. Everyone must have seen enough of this. Therefore, our urban and rural banks should change their faces and do things in a practical and realistic way. It is not allowed to do the trick of hanging sheep's heads and selling dog meat again. In this regard, we put forward the following principles:

Urban and rural banks should operate purely economic business, not sell public bonds, not sell lottery tickets, and not participate in any speculative business.

Urban and rural banks should be the bridge between urban funds and rural capital financing. It itself raises funds from national banks or general commercial banks and flows into rural areas, earnestly doing the work of returning funds to agriculture, and acting as an agent for urban banks to invest in rural areas.

Urban and rural banks should become the leaders of rural business activities. It follows the principles of economy and helps the development of the most economically favorable business in a certain area. It itself leads the countryside and implements a part of the national economic policy.

Urban and rural banks themselves are the backing of cooperative accounting. Its loans should be mainly for cooperative societies. Loans for improper purposes by local gentlemen and tyrants are the main target. Loans for improper purposes by local gentlemen and tyrants should be rejected in all cases. At the same time, it should use its power to help other financial institutions in rural areas. It should give substantial assistance to pawnshops and small money shops.

Urban and rural banks themselves should consolidate their credit and repel the intrusion of all evil forces, so as to become a general meeting of local funds, so as to change the trend of funds escaping into cities. For deposits and small savings, there should be specific guarantees, so that people have confidence in local financial institutions, and funds can stay within the local scope.

4. Relationship with National Banks

Urban and rural banks should not have relationships with local silver and regional——provincial banks in various places. Based on our current situation, it is simply difficult to find a healthy bank in many provincial banks. Therefore, urban and rural banks should directly contact national banks. It itself is the agent for the country to direct rural financial activities. National banks can use it to implement low-interest policies and suppress usury in rural areas. National banks can expand credit to it and stimulate domestic prices to balance urban and rural prices. National banks can use his activities to change the direction of capital flow and realize the country's economic policies. Therefore, in our opinion, urban and rural banks should be directly controlled by national banks and become a branch of the national bank's capital operation.

5. Organizational Unit Issues

Urban and rural banks should be organized according to the economic environment. The areas it includes should be based on economic units and should never be the same as political oppression. Because it is an economic organization, not a political institution. And special urban and rural banks can be organized due to the special economic environment of the place. Its form, its scope, its strength, can be changed according to the local economic situation, and there is no need to be consistent. The situation in various places is different, and it is absolutely impossible to force various places to adopt the same method. As for its capital strength, it should be determined according to the local economic development. The scope should not be too small. If the scope is too small, it is not enough for a money shop to operate, and there is no need to set up a bank. In short, regarding the unit issue of the establishment of a face-to-face rural bank, we believe that the following principles should be followed.

The urban and rural areas should be based on the economic environment and do not need to be in line with the political scope. Seeking an economic unit that is self-contained and active, regardless of others.

The so-called urban and rural areas should not be too small. If the scope is too small, the bank's strength will be weak and it will feel powerless.

Regarding organization, it can be changed according to the special economic environment of the place, and there is no need to adhere to the same form throughout the country.

6. Guarantee Issues

One of the most difficult points in running local financial undertakings is the destruction of local politics. The ravages of warlords and the extortion of local financial authorities are the main reasons for the bankruptcy of inland finance. Now we want to organize urban and rural banks. To hope that he fulfills his mission, we must first discuss the issue of guarantees. The state should issue a clear order to strictly prohibit local financial authorities from having relationships with such banks. These banks should strictly determine that they are supra-political organizations. No government agency can force it to accept debt certificates or borrow money from it. All losses caused by political issues, debt certificates cannot be forced to borrow money from it. The state should be directly responsible for losses caused by political issues. Banking operations are based on credit. If credit is damaged, all activities cannot proceed. Therefore, guaranteeing bank credit is a prerequisite for the healthy development of this system. And the proper way to guarantee is to isolate this kind of bank from the relationship with local finance. Most of the suggestions we made earlier are for this purpose.

Restore new transactions and cancel the submission of existing products.

The Huashang Securities Exchange received an order from the Ministry of Finance the day before yesterday, ordering it to open as usual on the 17th. For this reason, the exchange brokers convened another general meeting at 2 pm yesterday. Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 156

— (Xiao Bai)

If a person does not have adequate reserves and preparation in terms of ability, they will certainly encounter failure in the battles of life.

Young people are strong in character and have no fear of shrinking back. Therefore, their emotions are easily impulsive and their courage is great. They can bravely move forward, disregard everything to implement their ideas, and spare no sacrifice. Middle-aged people gradually become more worldly-wise and their youthful spirit diminishes. However, they are rich in the ability to observe and judge matters. Reason and emotion are both highly developed. Therefore, if these two can be properly harmonized, what a great force that would be!

In the youthful stage of life, what we need is the accumulation of intelligence, physical strength, and critical ability. Because if you don't put something in at this time, then you will not be able to get anything out of your life in the future. This is just like how we cannot withdraw money from the bank if we have not deposited money into it.

Old General Ding Huai 157

— Qing Qu

Old General Ding Huai, who defeated the French army at Liangshan, lived during the Guangxu reign of the former Qing Dynasty (the Sino-French War). It has been nearly fifty-two years since then, and few know his name. Previously, I saw reports that the National Government had issued an order to "commend and comfort" him. I understand that he passed away in Ping on the afternoon of June 24th last year, at the age of ninety-seven. The old general, who bore a generation of heroic name, should not be forgotten.

Looking back at the time when the French army attacked Liangshan, Liu Yongfu, a former general of the Taiping Army, had just been recruited by the Qing court and given the title of governor. Liu recovered the three provinces of Xuanguang, Xinghua, and Shanxi in Vietnam. Before long, Liangshan was disturbed, and Su Yuanchun, Pan Dingxin, and others fought hard but could not defend it. Fortunately, Ding was present and achieved the victory at Xiaonanguan. People only heard of the brave and selfless efforts of the generals Feng Zicai and others, but they did not know that Ding was also instrumental in repelling the enemy for over two hundred li in eight days and nights.

Ding was from Heqing County in western Yunnan. When Du Wenxiu's rebellion broke out, Cen Yuying, the governor of Yunnan, recruited soldiers to quell it. Ding was still young and plagued by hunger and cold, so he joined Cen's command. Cen considered him useful and soon appointed him as the general in charge of Tengyue, and later as the commander of Guizhou. Eventually, he was promoted to commander-in-chief of Jiangnan, but was later impeached by censors and left his post to live in seclusion. During his time in retirement, he spun yarn and wove cloth somewhere, but stopped due to financial losses. When Li Jingxi arrived in Yunnan, Ding was able to serve as an assistant in the local militia. Later, due to an increase in salt prices, he was dissatisfied with public opinion and was squeezed out. Later, when Cen Chunxuan was in Guizhou, he was recommended as the Zhen General of Zuojiang. Before long, he was promoted to brigadier general and concurrently served as the director of Longzhou. Until one year before the founding of the Republic of China, he was again dismissed from his post due to a case and sank into Hubei Province. Since then, his name was no longer heard in the officialdom.

In Hubei, he was known to Military Governor Chen Huilong, who ordered the Jianghan Customs to investigate a certain matter. Ding was greatly embarrassed, but was spared with the help of someone. When the Wuhan Uprising broke out, he had no choice but to lead his family to float down the river and take refuge in Shanghai. Unexpectedly, in May of the first year of the Republic of China, his enemies secretly broke into his room in the middle of the night near Jing'an Temple, killed his son and daughter-in-law, and were still not satisfied, and set fire to his house. Ding then moved north and lived a wandering life for over twenty years. Now, I hear of his passing, and the old general, who lived to be a hundred years old, has his merits recorded and passed down in the canon. Ding is still glorified.

Talking About Zhongming Hooks 158

— Zheng Yimei

Those who keep birds must beautify their cages, and even the smallest hook must be crafted with extreme ingenuity. The so-called Zhongming Hook is indeed famous and precious. Zhongming's surname is Xu, and he is from Hubei Province. He originally practiced the craft of engraved knives, but later came to Shanghai and changed his profession to carving purple copper cage hooks. The fineness of his carvings is unmatched in the world. Those who see them cannot help but suspect that they are the work of ghosts and gods. The carvings include both words and paintings, and the inscriptions are complete, further distinguishing between civil and military themes. For example, a Zheyant furong (zebra finch) is a civil bird, and its cage has a civil hook. The carvings on the civil hook are nothing more than scenes from "Romance of the West Chamber" and "Dream of the Red Chamber." As for birds that are good at fighting, such as the yellow-headed bird, the hooks are carved with military events from the "Romance of the Three Kingdoms," never mixed up. The value of a hook was originally set at thirty-six gold, but Zhongming loves alcohol and spends his days drunk, rarely working. Before the carving is even half finished, it is already pawned. The bird owner eagerly wants to get the hook back and redeems it for him. However, it is pawned again and then redeemed again. By the time the work is completed and in hand, it has often cost around a hundred gold. Therefore, if someone on the market today parts with a Zhongming Hook, the price is also no less than a hundred gold, or even over two hundred gold. Zhongming is still alive today, but due to excessive eye strain, he can no longer see things clearly. Someone saw him in Yu Garden and said that he is an old man with a red nose, hunched over and decrepit. It is said that his son-in-law can continue his work. The son-in-law originally specialized in carving fine patterns on the mouthpieces of dry tobacco pipes in a pipe shop. Zhongming saw that his skills were promising, so he married his daughter to him. And after being instructed, the carving of hooks is also quite impressive, it is said.

Odds and Ends

Gleanings from the Nanshe Memorial Meeting 159

— Shengwu

On the evening of the former New Year's Day, I attended a dinner party for the Nanshe Memorial Meeting at the Tongyu Restaurant. Many of the attendees were writers and historians, and their accounts were full of fascinating anecdotes. Seeing this, I couldn't help but feel itchy, so I gleaned some observations to serve as a supplement to Spring and Autumn. On that day, during Mr. Liu Yazi's speech, the atmosphere in the entire venue was tense, and applause was incessant. When he reported that Mr. Cai Yuanpei had been publicly elected as honorary president, the crowd clapped even more enthusiastically. Finally, they shouted "Long live the Nanshe Memorial Meeting!" More than 150 attendees stood up and drank a large glass each. At this time, snow was falling heavily outside the window, and the ground was covered in a silver world, which was a wonderful embellishment to this grand event.

Someone asked Lin Gengbai to talk about his love history, and he could not refuse, so he stood up and said, "I have never been in love, so how can there be a history?" This sentence was like a breaking of the ice in an old essay, simple and direct. The friends in the audience responded with "You are too polite, you are too polite." Seeing that the momentum was not right, he immediately shifted his target and continued, "Everyone should know that this year is Mr. Liu's 50th birthday. Today, we will use flowers to offer to Buddha, and everyone will drink a toast to Mr. Liu to wish him a happy birthday." Sure enough, everyone was coaxed by him to stand up and drink a cup, but he left the stage like that.

Among the female guests, Ms. Lu Lihua was the most eloquent. In two jokes, several "Gai! Gai!" (covers) caused the audience to burst into laughter. Then, Mr. Zeng Xubai came out and said that he was from Changshu and should say a few words, because one of Ms. Lu's jokes was told in the Changshu dialect. Mr. Zeng stood up and said, "Yes, right!" The whole audience burst into laughter again, saying that it was "certified" as an "ancient edition."

Most of the people who attended that day were strong men from the southeast, but there were also some distinguished guests from the north. Among them was the elderly Mr. Yan Ganyuan, who spoke about the situation in the northwest. We listened to the old man's gentle cough, and it was as if we were in the middle of a vast grassland with withered grass and running cattle and horses, listening to the anecdotes of the Han Palace. Sitting with Guan Lao was an old man named Wu Banshan, who was from Hangzhou and was formerly known as Mu Shi Jushi. He and his wife, Lady Fengyun, compiled and printed "Lyrics of Famous Women of Past Dynasties." I saw his inscription, and I have excerpted a poem as follows: "Each of the group heroes turned into something new, and people of their own color are self-reliant. After listening to the duo singing under the flowers, Li Zhu Duanhe is worthy of matching Su Xin." The old man is also very fond of good deeds. The current sage, Mr. Ye Chuyi, is his fast son-in-law, it is said.

Mr. Hu Pu'an's lofty ambitions have not diminished slightly. The "What to Do Song" that he distributed at the meeting showed his tragic and generous intentions. He explained in his own words: "In the past, Gui Xuan Gong wrote the 'Eternal Sorrow Song', and since Pangu, everyone is a person who can be scolded, and everything is something that can be scolded. This is the so-called day of helplessness. As far as I know, the changes in the world are becoming more and more urgent, and those that can be scolded have all been scolded by Xuan Gong; Xuan Gong has never encountered the opportunity to scold them. Although Xuan Gong is in a day of helplessness, there are still things that can be helped; today is truly the helplessness of helplessness...". As for the lyrics, Mr. Liu Yazi has two absolute sentences, "Gifted in the same seat", as follows: "The country has fallen into the hands of dwarfs, and the altar still seeks the old alliance. Enduring tears and pretending to be happy, my business is over, how can I support my eyes and wait for the river to clear. Wine dragon and poem tiger thirty years ago, the sword heart and Xiao Xin have not turned into smoke. If you make a bold statement in Xinting, I, Yi Wu Jiangzuo, am still virtuous." The implicit words show a strong excitement, worthy of being the leader of the literati. Those who want to know about Liu's life and his recent feelings can see it in this.

Also, that night, I sat with a friend at the Dahua Ballroom and made another piece. Gifted to Mr. Song Huanggong: "Old heroes are full of sorrow, and it is difficult to tame the dragon's nature, still arrogant. The dream of Jin Ge Iron Horse Liaoyang, how can I leave the tenderness to old age in this hometown?" A poem given to Mr. Ren Weizhi: "Thirty-five years into a glimpse, holding the intestines with a mango corner drunk face red, European knife mellow wine blood of the battlefield, what can we do after we die?" After the dance, Ji Yun: "Into the arms of the weaving waist ironing electric waves, Yu Yan Wei halo tired Jiaoe, stroking the ring body is a casual thing, I do not believe that the return of the intestines is a lot of spirit." Thinking of a foreign friend, "Turning green and returning yellow with thousands of tears, it is difficult for the beautiful woman to check the period. The northern Hunan is very common, and the sorrowful He Liang Su Li poem." Passion bursts out, Qingli can be read.

Mr. Hu Huaichen also wrote two poems on the spot as follows: "Try the Qiong Yan in the spring lantern shadow, Bai Ye can also be at the rice also Dian. The pattern of several restorations survives other factions, and the characters of Yonghe are prepared by the group. The things in the eyes become traces, and the heroic feelings on the seat are like in the past. Who cares about the new wine in the old bottle, only laziness is good and does not need to be transmitted. (The last sentence borrows Shi Nai'an's words, and slightly changes a word.) Simple and thick, the poem is like its person. His original intention was only to be lazy and not to be transmitted, I am now making it public for him, please don't blame him.

Xiaoxi Heaven 160

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23: Striding around the room, delivering a grand talk to encourage a lawsuit; pouring out the jug, reminiscing about old friendships to forget suspicions

He didn't sit down; instead, standing, he raised his wine cup and said, "I'll drink it all in one gulp, leaving not a drop. Please watch me." Having said that, he raised the wine in the cup to his mouth and swallowed it with a resounding whoosh. Then, he turned over the inside of the forest, facing it outwards for comparison. Wang Shicheng also had no way to refuse and stood up to drink his cup dry as well. Jia Duocai bent over, put down his cup, and nodded repeatedly to the two men, saying, "Thank you, thank you. Just based on you two so readily giving me face, I will definitely tell the landlord to make many concessions on the land price." Having said this, he sat down, just as the waiter delivered the dishes, and he repeatedly offered food to the two Wangs. Bei Hai was constantly expressing his gratitude, feeling that he wasn't exactly an easy person to talk to. He was truly surprised that he was putting in so much effort to arrange things today. He still needed to be extra cautious in his words, and thus, he began to pay attention to him. Whenever Jia Duocai asked a question, he never gave a definite answer. When Jia Duocai had drunk about half his wine, he smiled at Bei Hai and said, "Does Mr. Wang know that Miss Zhu Yueying?" This sentence came out of Jia Duocai's mouth lightly, but Bei Hai's face turned red, and he was so frightened that his heart was pounding wildly.

Chapter 24: Weighing profit over beauty, the gunner relinquishes his love; high ambitions and healthy feet, the strong man ventures into the wilderness

Wang Beihai's feelings for Zhu Yueying were just a moment of pity; it couldn't be said to be love. As that moment of pity gradually deepened, he slowly added a little bit of concern. Beihai certainly didn't want anyone to know about this situation, and he didn't expect anyone to know. Now that Jia Duocai himself brought up Yueying, it seemed like Duocai already knew everything that he had done, which made him not know what to say. His face turned red, and he answered unclearly, "That...that...ah! I don't know her. However, there's a Mr. Cheng who's with her...it's not exactly that I know her; we just live in the same hotel, so I recognize her." Jia Duocai laughed and said, "It doesn't matter. Nowadays, social interaction between men and women is open. It's fine to make friends. What's so important about it?" Beihai lowered his head in embarrassment, raised his cup to take a sip, and then said in a low voice with a smile, "I didn't expect Mr. Jia to be so open-minded." Duocai laughed and said, "It's nothing. Within Tongguan, people might think this kind of situation is a bit strange. But in Shanghai, a woman doesn't even need to completely sever her marital relationship with her ex-husband to cohabitate with a man. And another man can openly go in and out with that woman without avoiding people." (403)

Small Spring and Autumn Weekly

Silence and Leisure 161

— (Wen)

There is a key to dealing with matters: that is, you need to be silent and free. If you are unable to avoid being frantic and at a loss, Mr. Zhang Jian of Nantong once said, "In order to be a human and do things, you must be able to be still in motion, and to be free in busyness, in order to have insight into things and be beneficial to yourself. This is not easy, but as long as you can endure, you will naturally see busyness as leisure and motion as stillness." This so-called "endurance" undoubtedly requires a kind of learning to cultivate a calm mind and a quiet heart in order to reach the point of "being able to endure."

Interesting "Spring" Character 162

— Yao Mingran

If you take the character "spring" apart, there are three ways to dismantle it, and now there are very interesting dismantlings below: "January 28th" The glorious anniversary in the spring season is also a day of grief. "March 8th" Thirty-eight days a month, although it is a dream, but maybe the future will become an unprecedented fact.

Humble Tiger Name 163

— Shen Chu

"To talk about tigers is to change color," the tiger is such a ferocious thing. You listen to the pronunciation of tiger cubs, the shape of the tiger character, heroic and vigorous, is indeed a hero. Adding it to anyone's head will not lose its power. Tiger squats, tiger looks, tiger generals, etc., are all imposing and unrepeatable. However, unexpectedly, "Miscellaneous Records of the Western Capital" records: "The Han Dynasty used jade as a tiger cub, as a urinal, and made the waiter hold it to follow the lucky ones." To make a dignified tiger general, succumb to the name of a urinal, is really a fall!

Rich Beggar 164

— Xu Xiaoting

Rich beggars are a common occurrence in the Jianghuai region. Jianghuai people have a superstition that if parents die at the age of eighty-one, the children and grandchildren must beg for food. In this case, the children and grandchildren should follow the trend and beg from a hundred families? This will exempt them from begging in the future. This is a truly ridiculous superstition. The other day, a wealthy family staged this kind of farce because their mother died. A family of six or seven people, wearing torn clothes, carrying baskets, and queuing up on the road to beg. They are used to living in a shifted atmosphere and nourished body. Once they make a fool of themselves, the expressions on their faces are extremely embarrassing. In fact, the death of parents has nothing to do with the poverty of their children and grandchildren. The foolish people disturb themselves, and the level of superstition of the Jianghuai people is indeed self-inflicted shame.

Discussion on the Abbreviation of Legal Tender 165

— Chen Yijin

There have already been two entries in this publication on the abbreviation of national currency. In the reporter's opinion, the national currency should be written as 法幣 (Fa Bi). Why? Because the government issues 法幣 (Fa Bi).

In our business community, abbreviations have become a habit, but the two characters "法幣 (Fa Bi)" have a lot of strokes, and many people feel that writing them is inconvenient. Therefore, I propose to use the character "沛 (Pei)" to represent "法幣 (Fa Bi)." First, writing it can be convenient, and second, it does not interfere with the character "洋 (Yang)."

You don't believe it,

Dare to swear a deep curse before God.
