I Envy Today's Youth 167

— Qingfen

Starting from My Childhood: The Development of Children's Literature

If we just speed up a bit, everyone has had a period of devouring news reporter novels, forgetting to eat and sleep. As for the content of the novels, and how much good or harm they would bring us, we had no time to consider, mostly because we lacked the ability to think about those things. For me, this period was from the ages of fourteen to seventeen, from the fourth grade of elementary school to the third grade of senior elementary school. I boarded at a county elementary school surrounded by rural areas, and the thirty or so classmates who boarded there were also young people obsessed with novels. The school absolutely forbade reading novels, but we were relatively enlightened, knowing that simply prohibiting it was useless; so, they specifically designated several kinds such as "Romance of the States" and "Romance of the Three Kingdoms," allowing us to read them in our spare time. The meaning was that, except for these designated kinds, reading was prohibited. But who cared? As long as one classmate brought a novel from home, it would immediately spread to the whole group in a secretive manner. Depending on the closeness of the relationship with the owner, it would be passed around. Often, the person reading the second book would be urged by the person reading the first, and the person reading the second would urge the person reading the third. Thinking about that silly energy now is quite amusing. What we worried about most was being searched and having them confiscated; at the same time, we enjoyed the satisfaction and happiness of "I've read it too" again and again—although this satisfaction and happiness, looking at it now, seems so pitiful.

Later, I myself stood lecturing students. Fortunately, the situation there had changed greatly. Vernacular Chinese had replaced the position of classical Chinese, and students were not only not prohibited from reading novels, but were also guided to do so. Many famous old novels replaced the position of "classics" and "commentaries" and were introduced to the desks of young people. For things that should not be read, there was also an active explanation of the reasons why they "should not" be read, no longer an arbitrary prohibition. At the same time, foreign fairy tales and stories were being introduced one after another. Mu Mutian's translation of "The Happy Prince and Other Tales" by Oscar Wilde, and Zhao Kangren's translation of "Alice's Adventures in Wonderland" were published one after another. The names of Hans Christian Andersen and the Brothers Grimm gradually became familiar to young people. China's inherent folk tales and legends also began to be collected and organized. Lin Lan's compilation of "The Stories of Xu Wenchang" and others were published one after another. On the one hand, Mr. Ye Shaojun's creative fairy tales—later collected in the two collections "The Scarecrow" and "The Stone Statue of the Ancient Hero"—were also published in the "Children's World" one after another. Following this, various bookstores published books written for young people to read. Almost all the works of Hans Christian Andersen, the king of fairy tales, were translated. Carlo Collodi's "The Adventures of Pinocchio," Edmondo De Amicis's "Heart" (Cuore)... Almost all the famous works that young people around the world should read and love to read, the young people of our China have the fortune to read.

However, our country is a world-renowned ancient country. The characteristics of ancient countries are the long history of culture and the unusually large number of superstitious and bizarre legends and stories. Young people, having the opportunity to read freely, swallowed many useful things as expected, but many superstitious and bizarre stories of gods and martial arts novels were also loved by them. At the same time, the newly emerging film industry specialized in catering to the low tastes of superstitious and bizarre old people, using absurd stories of immortal swordsmen like "The Adventures of a Beggar Soilder" to construct many films like "Burning of the Red Lotus Temple," one after another. We all know that the suggestive power and educational effect of movies on human life—especially the pure-hearted, very weak-willed young people—is absolutely true. After reading those novels and then using these movies to confirm them, the impact on young people is far beyond the reach of school education. And the perilous international situation, the precarious state of the country, young people see a little news from the school's wall newspaper, and hear a little alarming words from adults; they can't wait for that day: to succeed in forging a sword, return after attaining enlightenment, and with just a few simple strokes, transform this world of only power and no justice into a dreamlike fairyland.

As a result, many unfortunate things happened. Three fourteen- or fifteen-year-old boys from the same elementary school in Changsha disappeared. They took some money from home and left a water buffalo, saying they were going to Mount Emei in Sichuan to learn from a master. After the parents' panic and chaos, they finally found these three treasures at the wharf in Hankou on a ship to Sichuan. At the same time, similar things happened in Wuchang and Guangzhou, which were greatly recorded in the newspapers. I had a sixteen-year-old apprentice who was learning business in a shop; he usually liked to read novels very much, and since the year before last, he had abstained from meat and practiced vegetarianism. Last year, on the first day of the lunar new year, his colleagues in the shop took advantage of the holiday to go out and play, but he braved the sun, snow, and cold rain to go to the Guanyin Temple on Xianglu Peak, more than ten miles outside the city, to burn incense. Judging by his actions, he was already on the path of cultivation.

Because of these possessed-like facts, they once aroused the worries of the education authorities and the loud calls of educators, who launched a movement to clean up and disinfect children's books. It has always been the failure of adults to guide, the neglect of parents to pay attention, and the courage of social education institutions to be derelict in their duties that, after being stimulated by these facts, gave them the opportunity to reflect. After the efforts of all parties, the children were finally rescued from the poisonous atmosphere and demonic path. This was only two or three years ago. Therefore, children's books, since their free development, have also gone through such a dark period.

There has always been an unforgivable mistake in the concept of children's books. It is believed that the entire image of children's books belongs to literature: therefore, the topics depicted are literary, and the writing task is for literary artists. Leading children's books far away from life, as if children should always live in a non-realistic poetic world; instead, the actual phenomena and common sense of life that surround them every day are neglected completely. As a result, in addition to cultivating children into dream seekers who avoid reality, there is no attempt to understand life and improve life.

It is only recently that social sciences that explain the meaning of life and natural sciences that explore the phenomena of life have been appropriately woven together, interestingly depicted, and originally written into special books for young people to read. The kindness of the person who first attempted this kind of work to the young people of the whole world, I think, should not be below the person who invented the term "education." Unfortunately, in this old country where everything is backward, it is still not easy to find such fresh children's books.

Recently, the "New Youth" published by Kaiming Bookstore, judging by its main purpose, is to teach young people to "understand society, appreciate literature, and understand nature." It is attempting to introduce social sciences and natural sciences to young readers with the same importance as literature. Reading its inaugural issue, it is indeed doing so in these three aspects. This made me recall the pitiful state of my own childhood, and envy the young people living today. Although our childhood has passed, there are still our younger siblings and children. We should all recall the pitiful state of our own childhood, and what we could not receive should be compensated for by our younger siblings and children. This is how humanity has progressed. We don't need to grieve for our past selves.

I am now so grateful that I am about to shed tears, and I no longer have the time to write down the advantages of "New Youth" and what other hopes I have. Let others say it.

Reading "New Youth" Inaugural Issue, Part 1 168

— Wang Tianxiu

I recently bought the inaugural issue of "New Youth" at the Kaiming Bookstore. Perhaps it has a certain power to attract people. I maintained a strong interest throughout and finished reading it in one breath.

I dare not arbitrarily determine that all the youth publications in the country cannot catch up with the "New Youth," but at least I must say that it should be the most outstanding youth publication in the country in recent times. Among a large number of poorly made children's books, it appears particularly vibrant.

Empty compliments or condemnations are enough to obscure the facts and cause the value of the original intention to lose fair estimation. Therefore, the following should quickly speak truthfully based on the inaugural issue of "New Youth" itself.

The balanced allocation of quality and quantity is an obvious advantage that should be emphasized. In the "Editor's Note" of the inaugural issue, there are these few sentences: "...The mission of this magazine is to teach young people (1) to understand society (2) to appreciate literature (3) to understand nature..." I think, those who generally have educational responsibility for young people may not have any objections to these three points or favor one over the other, right? And what is gratifying is that the editors can use these three points as editing guidelines. Analyzing the works in the inaugural issue, in terms of social sciences, there are four articles such as "Youth Reading Room" and "The Yellow River Waters Come From the Sky"; in terms of natural sciences, there are twelve articles such as "The Words of the Moon," "The Secret of Seeing," and "Scientific News"; in terms of literature, there are six articles such as "Bird Language and Animal Speech" and "Young Printer." Although the number of articles in each category is not similar, the allocation is very balanced in terms of the length of each category. This proves that the editors do not favor a certain category. They see the "vitamins" needed by modern young people spiritually, and combine them in appropriate amounts to make this delicious and nutritious "spiritual food" and send it to young people. This is the success of the inaugural issue of "New Youth."

Secondly, the appropriateness of writing techniques is also an advantage of this magazine. Anyone with writing experience probably understands that writing a work for young people or children to read is not as easy as most people imagine; because it must also have psychological basis, or actual observation and experience of young people's lives, and even the selection of each word and phrase, and the combination of sentences, must all adapt to their imagination, comprehension, and center of interest. In the inaugural issue, like Ye Shengtao's "Bird Language and Animal Speech" and Feng Zikai's "The Adventures of a Small Banknote," these two fairy tales are very skillful in the creative techniques of children's literature. People are willing to read them attentively and put their innocent little hearts into the works, developing feelings with the characters in the works. Mao Dun's "Young Printer" is a long serialized novel, and only the beginning has been seen now, so it is not easy to talk about it. Ye Shengtao is not only a writer who has long enjoyed a reputation in the literary world, but I imagine he must also be an excellent composition teacher in school. His "Wen Xin" has long been welcomed by most junior high school students. In this inaugural issue, he wrote an "Article Exhibition," presenting Zhu Ziqing's essay, titled "Background," and he attached a guiding passage of more than two thousand words after the article. I believe that this kind of sincere and unwearying explanation and instruction will not bore a young person who loves literature. This kind of emphasis on the essential nature of literature and intimate guidance is necessary for young people who are just understanding literature. Works on natural and social sciences should emphasize reasoning a little bit, but it is best to avoid preaching and lecturing writing methods. Most of the works on natural and social sciences in the inaugural issue can be said to be easy and light, and contain a bit of fun. Moreover, the editors are very good at using current events and things that are close to young people's lives as research topics. The topics taken from current events include Ding Xiaoxian's "The Yellow River Waters Come From the Sky," which explains the roots of the Yellow River disaster and the fundamental methods of treatment; Song Yi's "The Words of the Moon," which uses the style of Hans Christian Andersen's fairy tale "The Words of the Moon" to explain the news published in the newspaper that there will be two lunar eclipses this year and that British astronomer Jeans predicted that the moon would split. This kind of common sense topic can very well adapt to the curiosity of young people.

Deficiencies are not absent, but there are not many and they do not cause significant damage. For example, the historical story "The Song of the Striking," in the inaugural issue, although it is not very bad, and it contains a hidden power to inspire temperament, it is best to understand the social background at that time before appreciating historical stories, so that it is easy to deeply appreciate them. It is a question whether most young people have relatively sufficient knowledge of history and geography; of course, how much influence historical stories have on young people is also a question. If these pages could be used to publish a short story that is close to the real life of young people, it might be more eye-catching. The paper seems a bit too thin. It would be best to use the opposite cover to select and print some paintings or photographs worthy of sinking, I think these should also be loved by young readers, right?

"We want to develop comfortably, grasp the glorious future! We want to move forward smoothly, returning to that vast ocean!" This is a line from the opening song in the inaugural issue of "New Youth." I also hope for this vibrant youth publication.

Mr. Wang Tianxiu mentioned historical stories, and we seem to have a few words to say.

The purpose of publishing this type of historical story (or historical sketch) in "New Youth" is threefold: First, to write the rigid historical story a little more active, hoping to arouse young people's interest in reading history books; to put it exaggeratedly, hoping to arouse young people's interest in studying history. Second, hoping that young people can avoid getting a little historical knowledge outside of the "textbooks." Third, hoping that young people can understand the social background at that time from this type of historical story.

Speaking of the third point, our views are exactly the opposite of Mr. Wang's: Mr. Wang believes that "one must first understand the social background at that time before it is easy to deeply appreciate it," and we believe that one must understand the social background at that time from this type of historical story.

We believe that if a historical story is written in a way that does not allow young people to deeply appreciate it, it is a failure in the selection of materials or techniques, not because history is not close to real life, which reduces its "influence on young people."

We thank Mr. Wang for his enthusiastic guidance and criticism, and at the same time, we are willing to listen to the opinions of other readers.

New Youth Magazine

Part 2 169

— Qingshui

"Children's Year" has slipped past for a few months, quietly and silently, and no one is seen shouting anymore. Just for the "spiritual food" for children, good newspapers and good publications have been silent for a few months, without any interest at all. Only knowing how to "shout" but not knowing how to "do," such a "Children's Year," not to mention that the time is one year, even if it is extended to ten years, it will be useless. Can it provide salvation to the poor children who are in a bad environment, receiving a bad education, and are lost in the maze of bad publications? No, not at all. However, in the midst of these few months of boredom and disappointment, we were happy to read the "New Youth" semi-monthly magazine published by Kaiming Bookstore on January 10th. This is a general publication for children and elementary school students to read. The size is similar to the previous "Youth" (monthly) published by the Commercial Press, but the content has greatly improved; compared with the children's magazines sold in the market at the same time, it is equally easy for children to read and is also the most beneficial publication for the "physical and mental cultivation" and "academic cultivation" of children. Although I have passed my childhood, when it came into my hands, I felt the richness of the content and the clarity of the text, and I read it in one breath. It is rare to see such a good children's publication—at least that's how I feel personally.

Let's count the contents of the "inaugural issue." Youth Reading Room, fairy tales, scientific features and experiments, astronomical stories, art stories, article exhibitions, scientific world... these texts are all what every child or young person should read. Each text is written with the psychology and mood of a child or young person, so it is wonderfully clear, guiding, lively, and easy to read. Not only fairy tales, but also news and science are easy to understand, with no obscurity or dryness. It is impossible to obtain such a publication that seems to be written by children themselves ten years ago—even five years ago. When we read Hendrik Willem van Loon's "The Story of Mankind" in the past, we hated that we could not find a popular and interesting science book to read in China, and we almost wanted to change our nationality and become a foreigner. Now, after reading "New Youth," I hate that I was born too early and could not enjoy such a nutritious and easy-to-swallow and easy-to-digest publication in the golden age of childhood.

To put it more practically, most of the texts in here are written by famous experts and scholars, so it is of course good. Regarding literature and seemingly purely literary works, "Bird Language and Animal Speech," "The Adventures of a Small Banknote," "The Song of the Striking," and "Young Printer" can be considered the most noteworthy works with thought, content, and power. The progressive increase of the era in "Bird Language and Animal Speech" is very clear, and the underlying meaning is cool and delicious. It is a fairy tale, a novel, and a fable. Among the many fairy tales written by Mr. Ye Shengtao, I think this is a masterpiece that can best bite into the reality of the current turbulent era! I hope everyone will pay attention to reading such a good article and not let it go lightly. "The Song of the Striking," the story is old, but it is equipped with national consciousness, so that it reappears with a new posture and a new soul for children to read; this tragic and passionate historical story, which is enough to inspire, is also a very beneficial tonic in today's country, where difficulties are accumulating and spirits are fading. Feng Zikai's "New Year," writes about art in a smooth and moving way, like a story. Once you get it in your hand, you have to read it in one breath, and it can also be said to be a good work. Other scientific texts, such as the works of Gu Junzheng, Jia Zuzhang, and Jin Zhonghua, come from experts and are equally mature and attractive, making you feel unusually relaxed and happy after reading them.

Finally, I want to say this solemnly, although "Children's Year" has slipped past for a few months in a calm manner, but with this "New Youth," it can be considered that there is some contribution and it has not been wasted. I hope that "New Youth" will shoulder the responsibility of saving the children, enrich the content, and publish regularly with a new attitude, and that the children will always enjoy this good food and beautiful sacrament as much as possible! I also hope that all the children will accept this food and sacrament that is most beneficial to you, and sincerely and continuously enjoy it...

Number Three 170

— Xiao Shune

The warm sunshine sweeps away the frozen hues from the horizon, and the spirit of spring descends upon the human world: this is the vitality of a glorious future! "New Youth," we will joyfully watch it sprout tender branches, grow fresh green leaves, and bloom splendid flowers: life is filling our garden!

Yingying and I are together holding a copy of the inaugural issue of "New Youth," casually flipping through it to Mr. Shengtao's "Bird and Beast Language," reading along with a simple mood: the author's simple descriptions give me a deep intoxication! Look: "The bronze statue is of a man on horseback, wearing a military helmet, with two upturned mustaches, an arrogant and conceited appearance. The sparrow said, "What is this thing? Let's take a look." Saying that, it stopped on the military helmet of the bronze statue. The squirrel nimbly climbed up the body of the bronze statue, stopping only at the part of the mustache on the right, and he also raised his tail upwards. Looking from below, one only felt that the bronze statue had missed a shave when trimming his mustache." This kind of playful and innocent narrative is very much in the spirit of a child, finding the elements of true poetry in it; I am immersed in the beauty of this poem, feeling exceptionally relaxed! Although it contains the contemplation of children, it is aimed at a clear understanding of the real society. It evokes for us the hypocritical appearance of general feudal relics, and points out to us: "(The sparrow said): "Yesterday I went out for a stroll and flew to the front of that educator's house and saw him writing an article with his head bowed. ... It turned out that he was writing a primary school textbook for humans, saying that primary school textbooks often contain bird and beast language, letting primary school students associate with birds and beasts, ... inevitably making their thinking unclear and their behavior improper, no different from birds and beasts." But "if humans associate with us, does that humiliate them? Are our thoughts particularly unclear, and our behavior particularly improper? Are their thoughts not unclear, and their behavior not improper?" Look! How cleverly sharp is this sarcasm! I have unconsciously felt that the fairy tale art expressed contains poetic innocence, but is full of pity and disgust for mankind! Let the squirrels scold: "Humans are really confused and arrogant things!" Because the inferiority and cruelty of humans have provided them with powerful examples. All "municipal government matters that are judged before finding examples are called arbitrary; this is not very appropriate." The author repeatedly earnestly reminds: "We must look for examples." Everything must be thoroughly investigated in order to increase knowledge and experience." It is indeed an excellent lesson for young people.

Mr. Zikai's "The Adventures of a Small Banknote" possesses the same significance. The story is about Zhu Rongsheng picking up a banknote at school. He spent a lot of effort hiding it, and later went back to give it to his mother for buying rice for dinner, but his mother told him: "Ah Rong! This must have been lost by your classmate. You should give it to the teacher and return it to the owner. How can we use it?" The gentle words harmonize with the solemn thought, making people yearn for the purity of maternal love when reading it!

Mr. Mao Dun's "Little New Year Printer," although only the beginning of the story, the truthful narrative about the protagonist Zhao Yuansheng, especially the psychological description, gives the reader an indelible and deep impression. When he turned back and "Zhou Jiafu stepped on the rickshaw," whistling and calling Zhao Yuansheng to come to the car, he "stretched out a middle finger and waved it in Zhao Yuansheng's face, laughing wildly and shouting: "Nothing -- treating you -- haha!" Zhao Yuansheng's face suddenly turned red, and then turned white again." The brazenness of a wealthy young man and the shame felt by a poor child after being ridiculed are clearly displayed before our eyes, forming the opposition of two different social strata! When Zhou Jiafu asked the rickshaw puller to open his schoolbag and give Zhao Yuansheng something, "How can I accept things from others in front of the rickshaw puller? I would rather die than take it!" Zhao Yuansheng thought fiercely in his heart, and his face flushed." However, before the fundamental transformation of the current social conditions, such contradictory psychological phenomena are unavoidable for everyone. Perhaps this is the key to the development of the story.

Mr. Song Yunbin's "Song of Sorrowful Striking" is a historical account of Jing Ke's assassination of the King of Qin. The author uses a "historical eye" and agile techniques to extract a section of Jing Ke's preparation to go to the Qin state, rendering it with a modern spirit and transforming it into a new creation. The portrayal of the personality of a historical figure is the most delicate, without any exaggeration. Like: ""If the Crown Prince treats me like this, then killing the King of Qin is like killing a dog!" Dog Butcher Jia said excitedly." ""When you see the King of Qin, just treat him like a dog, and you won't panic." Butcher Jia said with a smile." The rough form of a dog butcher is portrayed extremely vividly! Also, like: "The current situation is very serious... Mr. Tian died at this time, it is always related to the current situation." Being able to put himself in the place of the ancients and use a tragic tone to depict the tense situation at the time, the writing is vivid and colorful. At this time of declining national spirit, I believe it is indeed a stimulant for young people.

In the story, the principles of art are incorporated. Mr. Zikai's "New Year Greetings" is of great help to the appreciation of art. Mr. Shengtao's "Article Exhibition" precisely analyzes famous works, from which we know the principles of the composition of literary and artistic works. Summarizing the activities of mankind, there is Mr. Jin Zhonghua's "The Power of the World." Explaining natural phenomena and their causal relationships, there is Mr. Song Yi's "The Words of the Moon" and Mr. Ding Xiao's "The Yellow River's Water Comes from the Sky." Others, such as Mr. Jun Zheng's "Flight Recorder" and "The Secret of Seeing," melt scientific theories into the furnace of literature, allowing them to appear in a light and graceful posture, without "distorting" the facts. Mr. Jia Zuzhang's "The Master of Antarctica - The Penguin" and Mr. Keshi's "Animals Wandering on the Crossroads" are masterpieces of scientific essays. In addition, the "Youth Reading Room" systematically and concisely reports the current affairs of the past half month, which is simple and pleasing.

Indeed! The content of "New Youth" is extremely rich. I want to affirm that this is the most desirable youth reading material of 1936!

What I Hope for "New Youth" 171

— Chen Qiyi

Being able to "appreciate literature and art, understand nature, and understand society" is really not an easy task. However, we grow up in this era, and we cannot fail to understand this knowledge related to practical life. Therefore, no matter how difficult it is, we must try our best to enlighten our understanding. However, it is not very good to rely solely on our own exercises, and we must also rely on advanced people to take on the responsibility of guidance. In this way, we can prevent ourselves from being confused by some erroneous views and falling into a dangerous situation during the exercise period.

The "New Youth," which appeared in a brand-new posture, can be said to be produced to meet our needs. After reading the inaugural issue, I was very satisfied because such youth reading materials cannot be considered anything but progressive. Recently, the "New Youth Society" is soliciting readers' opinions, so I wrote down my hopes for "New Youth":

(1) In the inaugural issue, I feel that there are too many articles about natural science. Although natural science is also very important, and the works are written in a very popular and interesting way, without any dryness, I hope that it is best to strive for an average amount of the three types of articles "Literature and Art," "Social Science," and "Natural Science" in each issue, avoiding focusing on one subject.

(2) I hope that "New Youth" can publish more research methods for various disciplines. Because learning with a purpose is extremely dangerous, and this kind of article is no different from the stepping stone to explore the path. In addition, if possible, it is best to answer various questions for readers for a long time.

(3) At this time, everyone who has awakened is concerned about the current situation. Therefore, lively current affairs issues need to be studied extremely. I hope that "New Youth" can also take this into account and conduct more detailed analysis and research on current affairs trends.

These three points are my opinions for the improvement of "New Youth."

The last point is that I hope that the editors of "New Youth" can take responsibility and guide young people to embark on a new path. On the one hand, we must strive to enrich the content of the publication, so that this "New Youth" can become the eternal friend of the vast youth group!

These are my current hopes for "New Youth."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Want Money, Not Life 172

— Meng Ruo

According to reports, a certain hospital in the French Concession recently, in order to imitate European and American blood transfusion treatment, specifically published an advertisement seeking blood donors. The age limit is 18 to 30 years old, regardless of gender, anyone can apply. Applicants must first undergo a physical examination and blood type test, and then be notified to draw blood on time and given a considerable blood fee. The number of people is limited to six per day. It is reported that many people have gone to apply in recent days, most of whom are unemployed, aiming to get some price to maintain their lives for a few days.

Selling blood to maintain life is indeed a sad situation. However, in today's society, except for a very small number of parasites who do not work for a living, most people rely on selling their brainpower or labor to make a living. Selling brainpower or labor is also a difficult task. But there is still a group of people who have brainpower or labor to sell but cannot find an employer. Their situation is even more difficult, being ostracized from the circle of life, crying for hunger and cold, and struggling with the demons of life. Therefore, a group of unemployed people are eager for work, as frantic as hungry dogs looking for food. As long as there is food to eat, no matter how difficult the job is, even if it kills their own lives, they are willing to take on the task. Selling blood is of course very pitiful. Blood is the source of life, and the most indispensable treasure of the human body. We absorb nutrients every day in order to replenish blood. Who would be willing to sell blood? But what if you don't sell it? Starving is more uncomfortable than drawing blood, even though the price obtained from selling blood is at most enough to maintain a few days of life.

It is said that there are blood sellers abroad who specialize in drawing blood for people. However, this is limited to a kind of particularly strong person, even if they draw blood, it will not harm their health. In recent years, hospitals in our country have also often adopted blood transfusion therapy, so advertisements for seeking blood donors are often seen in the newspaper. And every time the result of the solicitation is that applicants flock in, vying to be the first. A year ago, the wife of a friend of mine had surgery in a certain hospital, and the doctor also used blood transfusion to treat her. At that time, there were more than 20 people who came to apply. Later, a rickshaw puller was considered lucky (in fact, the most unfortunate) to qualify, and the rest went back disappointed. Five hundred cubic centimeters of blood was drawn, and the price was fifteen yuan. The doctor told him to eat more spinach and pig liver when he went back to nourish his body, and he needed to rest for three to five days before it would harm his health. But how did he answer? He said thank you for your kindness, to be honest, I can't afford pig liver. A family of four, this fifteen yuan, I must use sparingly and eat sparingly, at least maintain two or three months of life, and it is inevitable that I will suffer from hunger again.

Are they wanting money, not life?

On the Road to Climbing Zhuazhua Creek 173

— You Qi

Today, it is another poisonous day! Standing at the intersection at the other end of Guanyin Bridge, looking at the sun tightly hidden behind Dongshan Mountain, I felt a chill in my heart. But in the scheduled itinerary, today, in the evening, we need to rest in Songkan Town.

—Let's go, it's not early, the sun has already passed the top of the mountain! The porter shouted, his rough and hoarse throat like a broken gong.

—It's fifteen miles uphill to Datianjiao!

Fifteen miles is simply nothing in the boundless fields, and the porter's strong legs are so fast that they arrive in an unintentional moment. That is exactly the border between Sichuan and Guizhou provinces!

How is the provincial border divided? What are the obvious signs? I don't know, I only feel that there is a slight difference in the uniforms of the soldiers. Are people still wrapping their heads like that? The accents still contain the local dialect of Sichuan Province.

—Eat glutinous rice cake, come, the glutinous rice cake here is famous. Little Liu encouraged me, pulling me down from the pole.

The main ingredients of glutinous rice cake are a mixture of glutinous rice flour and some yellow rice flour. A broken iron stove with three cracks is roasting three or four cakes. The proprietress is over forty years old, and the wind and frost have deepened the wrinkles on her forehead. This unexpected business has aroused her surprise. Pull down the oilcloth curtain outside the pole, sit on it, let the mood calm down, and silently recite the rhythm of the rain.

Hotel Town, fill your stomach once, look, the rain has stopped, and dark clouds are still pressing down on the surrounding mountains. Porter Zhang squeezed over and said -- you still have to be careful ahead!

The shadows of last night immediately floated in my mind again. Isn't it, the wilderness is so quiet, even the sound of the bells of the donkeys carrying things cannot be heard, where to call for help?

—Old Zhang, is the front as dangerous as Jiupanzi?

He smiled, his expression simply extraordinary, shaking his hands, his head bent down with his waist. He told us that Guizhou Province is working hard on the construction of highways. When blasting along the mountains, the miserable cries of many monkeys fleeing were unbearable to see.

Walking, walking, on the winding path, slowly reaching the avenue that has not yet been officially completed at Xinwenguan. The road surface is not flat, and yellow mud and small gravel are laid on the entire road. After two hours, the mud is slippery, overflowing from the edge of the straw shoes into the soles of the feet, and the legs are heavier.

—Clap, clap, clap, clap,... The clear and crisp sound of the wheels hitting the mountain stones, shaking the dull air, followed by a boom, as if something had slid down, with a rustling sound.

—Did you hear that? This is the mountain opening work for building the road! Old Zhang said! Turn around the mountain corner ahead, and there is a bridge built, just at the end of the bridge! His finger drew a direction.

Standing on the bridge, underneath, if estimated in feet, there should be about twenty feet. The water, swirling, hit the rocks and splashed, embracing each other, and rushing downwards.

—Be careful! Hold on tight: the mud on the right mountain is slippery after the rain, don't fall into the slope! The three porters were so anxious, repeatedly warning, the blue veins on their foreheads were throbbing.

Really, this journey of twenty or thirty feet is a moment of life and death. The width is just enough for single guests to come and go. There is no shelter on the side. The mountain on the right is so high, and the little monkeys cleverly follow the sound of the bombing and run on it. But you can't look, maybe you will lose your life in a glance. The left side is even more unnecessary to mention, the shape of the cliff will make your legs weak.

Flower basket pole, carrying pole,... carefully passed, what about us, climb, grab, bite our lips, suppress the fearful mood, heart beating, ears roaring, the blood in the whole body rushing rapidly. Looking, almost all over, only Lao Tie is tightly pressing the sedan chair and is stepping into the entrance. In the sedan chair, there is an elderly man who has fallen asleep blankly.

—Slow down, don't pass, the worker looked at the already lit fire, desperately shouting but it was too late, Tie, they have already walked one-third of the distance. Go back? The retreat is even more difficult, it can't be done.

The medicine exploded, and the stones above rolled down like rain. The largest one looked like it was going to land on the top of the sedan chair. A sharp sword pierced many hearts, tightly covering their eyes with their hands, unwilling to let this terrible tragedy jump into their eyes.

How fortunate, the stone grazed the corner of the sedan chair and rolled down, the sedan chair swayed several times, without falling into the abyss. This should be attributed to the strength of the porters!

Breathing out a stuffy breath, we are discussing the way to reward them in tonight's lodging place.

A Scholarly Family 174

— Xu Ji

After the beginning of spring, the weather is still so cold: the wind pounces over the fields like a wild beast, pounces over the crops, pounces over the dead little town.

In the fields, it is as desolate as an ancient tomb; a few clusters of residual rice stalks are scattered and overturned on the dry and cracked ground -- that ground, in the prosperous era of the past, was also moistened by the sweat of their master's labor and the laughter and scolding of hope: "Damn it, look at this land, it's shiny, it's really good for making cakes"! -- but now, everything has become a light dream of the past. The sweat of hope and labor has been sucked dry, and people, like the rice stalks eroded by the frost and snow of winter, have withered and fallen, in the sharp and cold north wind, on the barren and dry ground...

The past is already past! Chongren Second Grandpa, shivering and wrapped in a dry and thin body inside a broken cotton robe that I can't remember how many years old it is, walked along the half-built highway leading to the little town, an indescribable sad feeling constantly playing a role in the gloomy sunlight; this role constantly aroused some nostalgic desolation, some declining and withering sorrow, and some other inexplicable resentment and sigh: "The good times are long gone, now it is... now it is... it's our turn to suffer. Scholars! Ha! Also considered a scholarly family. Now - what evil did the ancestors commit!"

It is a kind of shame! This shame endlessly just hit his heart like cold rain: Thirty years ago, wasn't his family still so glorious and prominent? Chongren Second Grandpa! Who in this small place doesn't know if you say it. The grandfather was a zhuangyuan, the father released two terms of daotai, and himself, was also received the "grace" of the country, and at a young age, he won the juren, and was also a "Jinshen."

It can also be said to be "showing off the ancestors and glorifying the clan," right? A large family, inherited from the ancestors, really began to vigorously "prosper" in the hands of Chongren Second Grandpa, bought fields, and built houses (in the house, there was also a plaque of "Imperial Gift" of "Zhuangyuan Mansion" passed down from the ancestors -- but now, the house has been torn down so that no trace can be found, and the original land has been built into the private residence of the nouveau riche with the surname Wang who "prospered" in the foreign goods business in Shanghai. And that plaque of "Imperial Gift" - Second Grandpa didn't dare to think about it anymore - maybe it had been chopped into pieces and thrown into the stove to be used as kindling, burned piece by piece...

Burned! The good days, like being thrown into the fire, have turned into ashes. The world suddenly changed its appearance, and people's braids were gone. Therefore, the reputation and prominence of his own family also disappeared day by day with the old world, like a strange dream, like a beautiful bubble.

"What evil did the ancestors commit?" I often think so. "Also considered a scholarly family," what kind of trick is this? Chongren Second Grandpa never understood it. Those fields, those houses, those servants, concubines, and those past glories that often appeared in dreams, passed by, all belonged to others. The age is getting older day by day, and the days are passing by in the situation of selling family property; now, everything is over, leaving only himself, a dying trunk, and this trunk is deeply containing the essence of opium.

I can't figure it out! Let's talk about his own two sons! Didn't they receive the education of "sages and sages" when they were young? But raised to be so big! Ha, one got a woman in the village, quietly like a wisp of smoke, I don't know where he is wandering: and the younger one? Damn it! Didn't someone come from Shanghai last year and bring such a letter: "Second Grandpa, your second young master is a robber in Shanghai and has been arrested and is going to jail!"

"What kind of world is this?"

It's over! Everything is over! The world has changed its appearance! "Scholarly children" will have to starve to death so silently (scholarly children still become robbers? Damn it! What evil did the ancestors commit!) What kind of world is this!

Thinking of his own such old age, "Juren" origin! Just now he went to the Zhang family, a nouveau riche family in the town with a little kinship, to "think of a way" and was even scolded by the people at the door! Thinking of the only two dry steamed buns he had eaten in the past two days, thinking that even the stolen "Japanese noodles" were about to run out! Walking on the half-built highway, Chongren Second Grandpa seemed to suddenly lose his balance, and suddenly squatted on the ground.

There was darkness in front of his eyes, he didn't feel anything: what he felt was just the past glory of his "scholarly family."

— (Fool)

The U.S. Treasury Department announced the other day that China has purchased gold worth 90 million yuan from the United States, which has been shipped out of the country with a special license. Tan Laosan said, Zhou Along, is destined to be poor, and picking up gold will turn into copper, sighing the uselessness of gold.

U.S. Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman Bidman spoke in the Senate, "severely criticizing Japan for dominating China and hindering U.S. trade rights, advocating strengthening naval and air forces, and not hesitating to fight Japan. Tan Laosan said, this song should only be found in heaven, how many times can it be heard in the world? A quick wit, should eat three cups of aged Shaoxing wine.

Broadcasting

Temptation: The Playwright's Broadcasting Company Has No Money for Radio Scripts (9) 176

— Written by Liu Yawei

A-Qiao, oh dear! The man has been washed away by the water!

Old Woman: What is to become of us! (Crying, shouting) Someone, please save our old man! (The sound of gongs gradually approaches, the sounds of people in chaos, the sound of water, the sound of wind, the sound of rain!)

Old Wang: (Shouting from that location:) Get on the boat! Get on the boat! Xiao Lu: A-Qiao, A-Qiao! Where are you? (Sounds of hurried footsteps)

Wang Da Niang, A-Qiao: We're here! Come quickly!

Xiao Lu, Old Wang, and others run quickly! Get on the boat! (Wind and rain intertwine) (Everyone rushes onto the boat)

A-Qiao: What about Big Brother? Xiao Lu! How could you forget Big Brother!

Xiao Lu: Alas! It's good enough that some survived!

Old Wang: I told him to fall back, but he insisted on leading the charge. The flood came so suddenly! Thirty or forty people, it was like a tiger swallowing flies, swept away in an instant.

A-Qiao: (Crying) Big Brother is dead too, my heavens! Can't you open your eyes and see who are the good people and who are the bad people?

Old Wang: And that bald Li, he was washed away by the water, but then he swam back. We thought he was incredibly lucky, a true escape from death. Who knew that in the second surge, he went to heaven with another thirty or forty people!

Old Woman: What? Our Baldy is dead too? (Crying loudly) My heavens! Isn't it enough that the old man died? Do you have to take Little Baldy away too? How am I supposed to live! I might as well die too! (Attempts to jump into the river)

Wang Da Niang: Li Da Ma, you have to think positively. People who are dead cannot be brought back to life!

Old Wang: Why do you want to commit suicide? At this point, we can only resign ourselves to fate! It's better to be alive than dead. (Wang Da Niang cries incessantly, the sound of a child crying, the noisy voices of people!) (Shouting) Xiao Lu, hold steady! Be careful with the oars!

Xiao Lu: Look! The flood is coming! Everyone hold on tight! (A great sound of water)

A: Everyone cries out in alarm for a moment! The sound of rain gradually diminishes, the sound of wind disappears Wang Da Niang: Li Da Ma is gone!

A-Qiao: Xiao Lu, all our belongings are gone!

Old Wang: Being alive is the only blessing! (The sound of oars rowing rapidly, the sound of rain still present, the sound of water very loud!)

Tanci (Storytelling with Stringed Instruments) 179

Xu Wenbi's Opening

Shiyin (1340) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

A slanting bridge leads into a courtyard, a stark chill rises. Silent, in the room, the treasure duck incense burner is damp. Regretful farewell and longing for spring, spring faintly illuminated. Encroaching on dreams, enough to dissipate the soul. I lazily do my makeup after waking from illness. Having drunk wine, I support my head, unable to restrain my thinness. Thinking of last night, the lamp flower continuously reported good news. But, the good times are shallow and unclear. Pleasantly, the parrot's intentions are heavy, its singing somewhat astringent. But, the swallow's heart is infatuated, complaining frequently. Already, the twenty-four seasonal winds and flowers send messages. Only the wandering silk threads and chaotic catkins are blocked by the gauze windows. I remember wandering through the garden, stepping over paths without end. A kind of affection is deeply engraved in my bones. I remember, comfortably, the study room is quiet with the curtain hook lowered. The sound of playing chess was sent from the depths of the hall. I remember, the thirteen mother-of-pearl pillars of the zither are selected. The jade ripples and pearl circles, truly the sound of white snow. I remember, secretly peeking from behind the screen, a smile on my face, secretly opening the way. The horse slips on the frost, walking under the moon. Now, I want to leave a conspicuous blade of grass on the riverbank. I will take my sorrow straight to the short and long pavilion. Only the dressmaking bees and butterflies are left, listless. Secretly buying rouge, embracing fallen flowers. Therefore, my gaze cuts off the green smoke and water by the bridge. The north of the magnolia hall tramples on the remaining spring. I resent the Eastern Emperor, spending all that thought.

Lu Qiuxia's Double Phoenix Pearls

Zhongxi (1040) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "The Jade Demise of Taizhen"

Since ancient times, beautiful women have had ill-fated lives. The news spreads that the lovely lady's soul has departed. In life, she pressed a book, a tribulation in the mortal world. In death, it is difficult to find her body after the tribulation. At that time, ten thousand miles of wind and clouds rose on the border. Lu Shan's soldiers mutinied in Fanyang City. Beacon fires filled the road to Hangu Pass. Approaching Chang'an, it was too uneasy. Therefore, the emperor was forced to flee to Sichuan. The Imperial Guards rallied to protect him. But who knew that General Weijia, Chen Wuli, was paying lip service and not advancing. The soldiers clamored and beat the drums wildly. But there was a sound of killing, swords clashing. First, the emperor's uncle and concubines were slaughtered. They also said, "If Yang Guifei is not killed, our anger will not be appeased." The king listened. The soldiers' hearts changed. Heaven and earth were turned upside down, and the ghosts and gods were alarmed. Making that Tang Dynasty emperor completely helpless. A shiver ran down his spine, his heart was in turmoil. He wanted to give up the beautiful woman. He did not care about the oath made on the Changsheng Hall. It was hateful that the government soldiers were so oppressive and violent. Their faces were ferocious, like tigers. Claiming to be the noble and precious Emperor. He could not, with all his heart, rescue a beautiful woman. Pitiful, Taizhen, with her jade-like and flower-like face. She was forced to commit suicide with a white silk. In an instant, jade was shattered, fragrance was extinguished, and her soul was cut off. Sad purple jade turned into smoke and dust. How can eternity be expressed? But, the dead beautiful woman will not be reborn. In the end, I, a stranger, have failed you. Don't say that the country is more important than the beauty. Pitiful, her beautiful face died under the pear blossom tree. Her fleeting smile was not destined to last. Today, with clear wine and fragrant brew, I offer a libation. The flowers are withered, the moon is waning, mourning her fragrant soul. The cuckoo cries blood with sadness, the candle burns to ashes, tears have fallen. Leaving me, unable to stop crying.

Upcoming Screening of "The Love History of Singing Partners" 181

Is Laurence Tibbett's Confession

Laurence Tibbett is currently the mainstay of the Capital Theater in New York. His nightly remuneration is three thousand US dollars. "Girl in Disguise" Yong'an Photography Notes 182

— Bai Mu

The Yihua Company's new sound film, "Girl in Disguise," written by Huang Ximo and directed by Fang Peilin, borrowed a scene from the Yong'an Company's photographic department store, one of Shanghai's three major companies, last night (the 15th). In addition to the full participation of more than 100 Yihua staff and actors, they also received enthusiastic assistance from Yong'an's colleagues, helping with the performance. It was truly an unprecedented event. The details are recorded as follows.

Not long after eight o'clock struck, Yihua's large team, loaded onto ten large trucks, marched in a grand manner, as if facing a formidable enemy. Cameras and a large number of props displayed their power in the magnificent building.

Preparations began, moving equipment, arranging lights, and setting up the camera. People surged like a tide, like the sun rising. Inside the entire Yong'an Company, only a multitude of heads moved, and thousands of shadows swayed. When the lights were turned on, the bright glass sparkled with gold, like a silver world, which was extremely beautiful. Each position did not stop for even a moment. By eleven o'clock at night, everything was arranged properly, and the filming work began actively.

The scene being filmed that night was Yuan Meiyun's return from Nanyang, led by her grandfather Wang Guilin to visit Shanghai's popular shopping mall. Because Yuan Meiyun was dressed as an elegant young gentleman, several modern girls flirted with her, which was a very exciting scene.

Twelve o'clock was the time for char siu buns. A thousand char siu buns were moved down from Dale. The staff finally took a short break at this point, wolfing down the buns to prepare for the next work.

The char siu bun time passed, and then filming continued smoothly with the hard work of everyone.

When the filming was completed, everyone cheered like triumphant soldiers. But at this time, the sky was already beginning to turn white in the east. The streets of the metropolis would be active again at seven o'clock. Ten large trucks carried this large group of people on the road of triumph. Facing the early spring breeze, everyone's faces were full of radiance, a kind of joy and comfort from a satisfactory job.

Lianhua Tidbits 183

The filming of "The Lost Lamb" is intensifying, and it should be completed by the end of this month. The last scene of Huacun has been set up, and filming will take place soon. Once the Huacun scenes are completed, the entire team will set off for Suzhou. When they return in triumph, it will be the day that "The Lost Lamb" is fully completed.

Both Fei Boqing and Hong Quan have always played villains in films. In "Lang Tao Sha," Fei plays a slick and treacherous husband who dies at the hands of Jin Xia. When filming this scene, Lao Jin swung his iron fist, and Fei Boqing, who was weak and frail, was not really beaten to death, but he was dizzy and almost lost consciousness.

Zheng Yingshi's young son, at the strong invitation of Cai Chusheng, made an appearance in "The Lost Lamb."

"Go to Nature" filmed a scene in a wooden house on an island. The season was midsummer. It was already difficult for the actors to work naked in the sweltering weather, but because of the plot, they also had to drag a fan and suffer from the cold wind. From our cold perspective, this wooden house on the island is simply an asylum for those with wind sickness.

Zheng Junli has changed his previous style in "The Lost Lamb." Zheng said: "I hope that I can be a versatile actor. The role I play in The Lost Lamb is my biggest attempt."

"Song of a Loving Mother" is the most spectacular film co-produced by all the male and female actors of Lianhua. Because there are so many actors in this film, the atmosphere on the set has been even more lively recently.

Key Roles in "Iron-Blooded General" 184

The Interesting Story of a Tall Husband and a Short Wife

Hollywood is truly a mysterious place. Many tall male actors on the silver screen are married to short wives. Let's examine the cast of "Iron-Blooded General" to understand this. In this film, there are three actors whose height exceeds six feet two inches. These three are the protagonist, and their wives are the smallest women in the film city. Ai Luoyu is only five feet tall and weighs less than one hundred pounds. Luo Ba Bala's wife is five feet one inch tall and weighs ninety-eight pounds. Alexander's wife is a famous actress and is taller, but is only five feet tall. Furthermore, "Iron-Blooded General" will be screened at the Da Guangming soon.

Preferential Rates for Children's Literature Subscribers 185

The Children's Literature Bi-monthly, published by the Children's Literature Society of Shanghai Beiguan Two Roads Sanle, is edited by children's book writer Lin Yin. Since its publication, it has been welcomed by readers everywhere. The twelfth issue has now been published, and the content is even more exciting. Now that the school year has begun, special preferential measures are being offered. All subscribers who pre-order twenty-four issues for the year and pay in advance will receive a discount of one yuan in national currency and will also receive a free book worth one yuan. Local subscribers can call 93546, and someone will be sent to discuss the matter.
